22// This header file defines implementation details of how the trace macros in
23// trace_event_common.h collect and store trace events. Anything not
24// implementation-specific should go in trace_macros_common.h instead of here.
25
26
27// The pointer returned from GetCategoryGroupEnabled() points to a
28// value with zero or more of the following bits. Used in this class only.
29// The TRACE_EVENT macros should only use the value as a bool.
30// These values must be in sync with macro values in trace_log.h in
31// chromium.
32enum CategoryGroupEnabledFlags {
33 // Category group enabled for the recording mode.
34 kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags = 1 << 0,
35 // Category group enabled by SetEventCallbackEnabled().
36 kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags = 1 << 2,
37 // Category group enabled to export events to ETW.
38 kEnabledForETWExport_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags = 1 << 3,
39};
40

64////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
65// Implementation specific tracing API definitions.
66
67// Get a pointer to the enabled state of the given trace category. Only
68// long-lived literal strings should be given as the category group. The
69// returned pointer can be held permanently in a local static for example. If
70// the unsigned char is non-zero, tracing is enabled. If tracing is enabled,
71// TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENT can be called. It's OK if tracing is disabled
72// between the load of the tracing state and the call to
73// TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENT, because this flag only provides an early out
74// for best performance when tracing is disabled.
75// const uint8_t*
76// TRACE_EVENT_API_GET_CATEGORY_GROUP_ENABLED(const char* category_group)
77#define TRACE_EVENT_API_GET_CATEGORY_GROUP_ENABLEDv8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController
() ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled \
78 v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController() \
79 ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled
80

306// TraceID encapsulates an ID that can either be an integer or pointer.
307class TraceID {
308 public:
309 class WithScope {
310 public:
311 WithScope(const char* scope, uint64_t raw_id)
312 : scope_(scope), raw_id_(raw_id) {}
313 uint64_t raw_id() const { return raw_id_; }
314 const char* scope() const { return scope_; }
315
316 private:
317 const char* scope_ = nullptr;
318 uint64_t raw_id_;
319 };
320
321 TraceID(const void* raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
322 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(raw_id))) {}
323 TraceID(uint64_t raw_id, unsigned int* flags) : raw_id_(raw_id) {
324 (void)flags;
325 }
326 TraceID(unsigned int raw_id, unsigned int* flags) : raw_id_(raw_id) {
327 (void)flags;
328 }
329 TraceID(uint16_t raw_id, unsigned int* flags) : raw_id_(raw_id) {
330 (void)flags;
331 }
332 TraceID(unsigned char raw_id, unsigned int* flags) : raw_id_(raw_id) {
333 (void)flags;
334 }
335 TraceID(int64_t raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
336 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_id)) {
337 (void)flags;
338 }
339 TraceID(int raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
340 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_id)) {
341 (void)flags;
342 }
343 TraceID(int16_t raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
344 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_id)) {
345 (void)flags;
346 }
347 TraceID(signed char raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
348 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_id)) {
349 (void)flags;
350 }
351 TraceID(WithScope scoped_id, unsigned int* flags)
352 : scope_(scoped_id.scope()), raw_id_(scoped_id.raw_id()) {}
353
354 uint64_t raw_id() const { return raw_id_; }
355 const char* scope() const { return scope_; }
356
357 private:
358 const char* scope_ = nullptr;
359 uint64_t raw_id_;
360};

372static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEventImpl(
373 char phase, const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
374 const char* scope, uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id, int32_t num_args,
375 const char** arg_names, const uint8_t* arg_types,
376 const uint64_t* arg_values, unsigned int flags) {
377 std::unique_ptr<ConvertableToTraceFormat> arg_convertables[2];
378 if (num_args > 0 && arg_types[0] == TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8))) {
379 arg_convertables[0].reset(reinterpret_cast<ConvertableToTraceFormat*>(
380 static_cast<intptr_t>(arg_values[0])));
381 }
382 if (num_args > 1 && arg_types[1] == TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8))) {
383 arg_convertables[1].reset(reinterpret_cast<ConvertableToTraceFormat*>(
384 static_cast<intptr_t>(arg_values[1])));
385 }
386 DCHECK_LE(num_args, 2)((void) 0);
387 v8::TracingController* controller =
388 v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController();
389 return controller->AddTraceEvent(phase, category_group_enabled, name, scope,
390 id, bind_id, num_args, arg_names, arg_types,
391 arg_values, arg_convertables, flags);
392}

394static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEventWithTimestampImpl(
395 char phase, const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
396 const char* scope, uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id, int32_t num_args,
397 const char** arg_names, const uint8_t* arg_types,
398 const uint64_t* arg_values, unsigned int flags, int64_t timestamp) {
399 std::unique_ptr<ConvertableToTraceFormat> arg_convertables[2];
400 if (num_args > 0 && arg_types[0] == TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8))) {
401 arg_convertables[0].reset(reinterpret_cast<ConvertableToTraceFormat*>(
402 static_cast<intptr_t>(arg_values[0])));
403 }
404 if (num_args > 1 && arg_types[1] == TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8))) {
405 arg_convertables[1].reset(reinterpret_cast<ConvertableToTraceFormat*>(
406 static_cast<intptr_t>(arg_values[1])));
407 }
408 DCHECK_LE(num_args, 2)((void) 0);
409 v8::TracingController* controller =
410 v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController();
411 return controller->AddTraceEventWithTimestamp(
412 phase, category_group_enabled, name, scope, id, bind_id, num_args,
413 arg_names, arg_types, arg_values, arg_convertables, flags, timestamp);
414}

416// Define SetTraceValue for each allowed type. It stores the type and
417// value in the return arguments. This allows this API to avoid declaring any
418// structures so that it is portable to third_party libraries.
419// This is the base implementation for integer types (including bool) and enums.
420template <typename T>
421static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) typename std::enable_if<
422 std::is_integral<T>::value || std::is_enum<T>::value, void>::type
423SetTraceValue(T arg, unsigned char* type, uint64_t* value) {
424 *type = std::is_same<T, bool>::value
425 ? TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_BOOL(static_cast<unsigned char>(1))
426 : std::is_signed<T>::value ? TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_INT(static_cast<unsigned char>(3))
427 : TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_UINT(static_cast<unsigned char>(2));
428 *value = static_cast<uint64_t>(arg);
429}
430
431#define INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(actual_type, value_type_id) \
432 static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) void SetTraceValue(actual_type arg, unsigned char* type, \
433 uint64_t* value) { \
434 *type = value_type_id; \
435 *value = 0; \
436 STATIC_ASSERT(sizeof(arg) <= sizeof(*value))static_assert(sizeof(arg) <= sizeof(*value), "sizeof(arg) <= sizeof(*value)"
); \
437 memcpy(value, &arg, sizeof(arg)); \
438 }
439INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(double, TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_DOUBLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(4)))
440INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(const void*, TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_POINTER(static_cast<unsigned char>(5)))
441INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(const char*, TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_STRING(static_cast<unsigned char>(6)))
442INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(const TraceStringWithCopy&,
443 TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_COPY_STRING(static_cast<unsigned char>(7)))
444#undef INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE
445
446static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) void SetTraceValue(ConvertableToTraceFormat* convertable_value,
447 unsigned char* type, uint64_t* value) {
448 *type = TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8));
449 *value = static_cast<uint64_t>(reinterpret_cast<intptr_t>(convertable_value));
450}
451
452template <typename T>
453static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) typename std::enable_if<
454 std::is_convertible<T*, ConvertableToTraceFormat*>::value>::type
455SetTraceValue(std::unique_ptr<T> ptr, unsigned char* type, uint64_t* value) {
456 SetTraceValue(ptr.release(), type, value);
457}
458
459// These AddTraceEvent template
460// function is defined here instead of in the macro, because the arg_values
461// could be temporary objects, such as std::string. In order to store
462// pointers to the internal c_str and pass through to the tracing API,
463// the arg_values must live throughout these procedures.
464
465static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEvent(char phase,
466 const uint8_t* category_group_enabled,
467 const char* name, const char* scope,
468 uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id,
469 unsigned int flags) {
470 return TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENTv8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEventImpl(phase, category_group_enabled, name,
471 scope, id, bind_id, kZeroNumArgs,
472 nullptr, nullptr, nullptr, flags);
473}
474
475template <class ARG1_TYPE>
476static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEvent(
477 char phase, const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
478 const char* scope, uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id, unsigned int flags,
479 const char* arg1_name, ARG1_TYPE&& arg1_val) {
480 const int num_args = 1;
481 uint8_t arg_type;
482 uint64_t arg_value;
483 SetTraceValue(std::forward<ARG1_TYPE>(arg1_val), &arg_type, &arg_value);
484 return TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENTv8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEventImpl(
485 phase, category_group_enabled, name, scope, id, bind_id, num_args,
486 &arg1_name, &arg_type, &arg_value, flags);
487}

489template <class ARG1_TYPE, class ARG2_TYPE>
490static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEvent(
491 char phase, const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
492 const char* scope, uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id, unsigned int flags,

494 ARG2_TYPE&& arg2_val) {
495 const int num_args = 2;
496 const char* arg_names[2] = {arg1_name, arg2_name};
497 unsigned char arg_types[2];
498 uint64_t arg_values[2];
499 SetTraceValue(std::forward<ARG1_TYPE>(arg1_val), &arg_types[0],
500 &arg_values[0]);
501 SetTraceValue(std::forward<ARG2_TYPE>(arg2_val), &arg_types[1],
502 &arg_values[1]);
503 return TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENTv8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEventImpl(
504 phase, category_group_enabled, name, scope, id, bind_id, num_args,
505 arg_names, arg_types, arg_values, flags);
506}

550// Used by TRACE_EVENTx macros. Do not use directly.
551class ScopedTracer {
552 public:
553 // Note: members of data_ intentionally left uninitialized. See Initialize.
554 ScopedTracer() : p_data_(nullptr) {}
7
←
3 uninitialized fields at the end of the constructor call
555
556 ~ScopedTracer() {
557 if (p_data_ && base::Relaxed_Load(reinterpret_cast<const base::Atomic8*>(
558 data_.category_group_enabled))) {
559 TRACE_EVENT_API_UPDATE_TRACE_EVENT_DURATIONv8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController
() ->UpdateTraceEventDuration(
560 data_.category_group_enabled, data_.name, data_.event_handle);
561 }
562 }
563
564 void Initialize(const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
565 uint64_t event_handle) {
566 data_.category_group_enabled = category_group_enabled;
567 data_.name = name;
568 data_.event_handle = event_handle;
569 p_data_ = &data_;
570 }
571
572 private:
573 // This Data struct workaround is to avoid initializing all the members
574 // in Data during construction of this object, since this object is always
575 // constructed, even when tracing is disabled. If the members of Data were
576 // members of this class instead, compiler warnings occur about potential
577 // uninitialized accesses.
578 struct Data {
579 const uint8_t* category_group_enabled;
uninitialized pointer 'this->data_.category_group_enabled'
580 const char* name;
uninitialized pointer 'this->data_.name'
581 uint64_t event_handle;
uninitialized field 'this->data_.event_handle'
582 };
583 Data* p_data_;
584 Data data_;
585};

42namespace v8 {
43namespace internal {

45namespace {
46struct WasmCompileControls {
47 uint32_t MaxWasmBufferSize = std::numeric_limits<uint32_t>::max();
48 bool AllowAnySizeForAsync = true;
49};
50using WasmCompileControlsMap = std::map<v8::Isolate*, WasmCompileControls>;
51
52// We need per-isolate controls, because we sometimes run tests in multiple
53// isolates concurrently. Methods need to hold the accompanying mutex on access.
54// To avoid upsetting the static initializer count, we lazy initialize this.
55DEFINE_LAZY_LEAKY_OBJECT_GETTER(WasmCompileControlsMap,WasmCompileControlsMap* GetPerIsolateWasmControls() { static ::
v8::base::LeakyObject<WasmCompileControlsMap> object{};
return object.get(); }
56 GetPerIsolateWasmControls)WasmCompileControlsMap* GetPerIsolateWasmControls() { static ::
v8::base::LeakyObject<WasmCompileControlsMap> object{};
return object.get(); }
57base::LazyMutex g_PerIsolateWasmControlsMutex = LAZY_MUTEX_INITIALIZER{ { 0 }, { {} } };
58
59bool IsWasmCompileAllowed(v8::Isolate* isolate, v8::Local<v8::Value> value,
60 bool is_async) {
61 base::MutexGuard guard(g_PerIsolateWasmControlsMutex.Pointer());
62 DCHECK_GT(GetPerIsolateWasmControls()->count(isolate), 0)((void) 0);
63 const WasmCompileControls& ctrls = GetPerIsolateWasmControls()->at(isolate);
64 return (is_async && ctrls.AllowAnySizeForAsync) ||
65 (value->IsArrayBuffer() &&
66 v8::Local<v8::ArrayBuffer>::Cast(value)->ByteLength() <=
67 ctrls.MaxWasmBufferSize) ||
68 (value->IsArrayBufferView() &&
69 v8::Local<v8::ArrayBufferView>::Cast(value)->ByteLength() <=
70 ctrls.MaxWasmBufferSize);
71}
72
73// Use the compile controls for instantiation, too
74bool IsWasmInstantiateAllowed(v8::Isolate* isolate,
75 v8::Local<v8::Value> module_or_bytes,
76 bool is_async) {
77 base::MutexGuard guard(g_PerIsolateWasmControlsMutex.Pointer());
78 DCHECK_GT(GetPerIsolateWasmControls()->count(isolate), 0)((void) 0);
79 const WasmCompileControls& ctrls = GetPerIsolateWasmControls()->at(isolate);
80 if (is_async && ctrls.AllowAnySizeForAsync) return true;
81 if (!module_or_bytes->IsWasmModuleObject()) {
82 return IsWasmCompileAllowed(isolate, module_or_bytes, is_async);
83 }
84 v8::Local<v8::WasmModuleObject> module =
85 v8::Local<v8::WasmModuleObject>::Cast(module_or_bytes);
86 return static_cast<uint32_t>(
87 module->GetCompiledModule().GetWireBytesRef().size()) <=
88 ctrls.MaxWasmBufferSize;
89}
90
91v8::Local<v8::Value> NewRangeException(v8::Isolate* isolate,
92 const char* message) {
93 return v8::Exception::RangeError(
94 v8::String::NewFromOneByte(isolate,
95 reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(message))
96 .ToLocalChecked());
97}
98
99void ThrowRangeException(v8::Isolate* isolate, const char* message) {
100 isolate->ThrowException(NewRangeException(isolate, message));
101}
102
103bool WasmModuleOverride(const v8::FunctionCallbackInfo<v8::Value>& args) {
104 if (IsWasmCompileAllowed(args.GetIsolate(), args[0], false)) return false;
105 ThrowRangeException(args.GetIsolate(), "Sync compile not allowed");
106 return true;
107}
108
109bool WasmInstanceOverride(const v8::FunctionCallbackInfo<v8::Value>& args) {
110 if (IsWasmInstantiateAllowed(args.GetIsolate(), args[0], false)) return false;
111 ThrowRangeException(args.GetIsolate(), "Sync instantiate not allowed");
112 return true;
113}
114
115V8_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT__attribute__((warn_unused_result)) Object CrashUnlessFuzzing(Isolate* isolate) {
116 CHECK(FLAG_fuzzing)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(FLAG_fuzzing)), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "FLAG_fuzzing"); } } while (false);
117 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
118}
119
120// Assert that the given argument is a number within the Int32 range
121// and convert it to int32_t. If the argument is not an Int32 we crash if not
122// in fuzzing mode.
123#define CONVERT_INT32_ARG_FUZZ_SAFE(name, index)if (!args[index].IsNumber()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate
); int32_t name = 0; if (!args[index].ToInt32(&name)) return
CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate); \
124 if (!args[index].IsNumber()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate); \
125 int32_t name = 0; \
126 if (!args[index].ToInt32(&name)) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
127
128// Cast the given object to a boolean and store it in a variable with
129// the given name. If the object is not a boolean we crash if not in
130// fuzzing mode.
131#define CONVERT_BOOLEAN_ARG_FUZZ_SAFE(name, index)if (!args[index].IsBoolean()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate
); bool name = args[index].IsTrue(isolate); \
132 if (!args[index].IsBoolean()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate); \
133 bool name = args[index].IsTrue(isolate);
134
135} // namespace

(__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled()
), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_DeoptimizeNow(args_length, args_object

; return (__RT_impl_Runtime_DeoptimizeNow(args, isolate)).ptr
(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_DeoptimizeNow(RuntimeArguments

199 HandleScope scope(isolate);
200 DCHECK_EQ(0, args.length())((void) 0);
201
202 Handle<JSFunction> function;
203
204 // Find the JavaScript function on the top of the stack.
205 JavaScriptFrameIterator it(isolate);
206 if (!it.done()) function = handle(it.frame()->function(), isolate);
207 if (function.is_null()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);

210 Deoptimizer::DeoptimizeFunction(*function);
211 }

259RUNTIME_FUNCTION(Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall)static inline __attribute__((always_inline)) Object __RT_impl_Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall

)) static Address Stats_Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall(int

timer(isolate, RuntimeCallCounterId::kRuntime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall
); static v8::base::AtomicWord trace_event_unique_atomic259 =
0; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled259
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled259 = reinterpret_cast
<const uint8_t*>(v8::base::Relaxed_Load(&(trace_event_unique_atomic259
))); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled259) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled259
= v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController
() ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled("disabled-by-default-" "v8.runtime"
); v8::base::Relaxed_Store(&(trace_event_unique_atomic259
), (reinterpret_cast<v8::base::AtomicWord>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled259
))); };; v8::internal::tracing::ScopedTracer trace_event_unique_tracer259
; if (v8::base::Relaxed_Load(reinterpret_cast<const v8::base
::Atomic8*>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled259)
) & (kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags
)) { uint64_t h = v8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('X')
, trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled259, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall", v8::internal::tracing::
kGlobalScope, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId, v8::internal::tracing
::kNoId, (static_cast<unsigned int>(0))); trace_event_unique_tracer259
.Initialize(trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled259, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall", h); }; RuntimeArguments
args(args_length, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } Address Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall
(int args_length, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { (
(void) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled
()), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall(args_length
, args_object, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(args_length,
args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_OptimizeFunctionOnNextCall
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
260 HandleScope scope(isolate);
261
262 if (args.length() != 1 && args.length() != 2) {
263 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
264 }
265
266 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, function_object, 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[0].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> function_object = args.at<Object>
(0);;
267 if (!function_object->IsJSFunction()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
268 Handle<JSFunction> function = Handle<JSFunction>::cast(function_object);
269
270 // The following conditions were lifted (in part) from the DCHECK inside
271 // JSFunction::MarkForOptimization().
272
273 if (!function->shared().allows_lazy_compilation()) {
274 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
275 }
276
277 // If function isn't compiled, compile it now.
278 IsCompiledScope is_compiled_scope(
279 function->shared().is_compiled_scope(isolate));
280 if (!is_compiled_scope.is_compiled() &&
281 !Compiler::Compile(function, Compiler::CLEAR_EXCEPTION,
282 &is_compiled_scope)) {
283 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
284 }
285
286 if (!FLAG_opt) return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
287
288 if (function->shared().optimization_disabled() &&
289 function->shared().disable_optimization_reason() ==
290 BailoutReason::kNeverOptimize) {
291 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
292 }
293
294 if (function->shared().HasAsmWasmData()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
295
296 if (FLAG_testing_d8_test_runner) {
297 PendingOptimizationTable::MarkedForOptimization(isolate, function);
298 }
299
300 if (function->HasAvailableOptimizedCode()) {
301 DCHECK(function->HasAttachedOptimizedCode() ||((void) 0)
302 function->ChecksOptimizationMarker())((void) 0);
303 if (FLAG_testing_d8_test_runner) {
304 PendingOptimizationTable::FunctionWasOptimized(isolate, function);
305 }
306 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
307 }
308
309 ConcurrencyMode concurrency_mode = ConcurrencyMode::kNotConcurrent;
310 if (args.length() == 2) {
311 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, type, 1)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[1].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[1].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> type = args.at<Object>(1);;
312 if (!type->IsString()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
313 if (Handle<String>::cast(type)->IsOneByteEqualTo(
314 StaticCharVector("concurrent")) &&
315 isolate->concurrent_recompilation_enabled()) {
316 concurrency_mode = ConcurrencyMode::kConcurrent;
317 }
318 }
319 if (FLAG_trace_opt) {
320 PrintF("[manually marking ");
321 function->ShortPrint();
322 PrintF(" for %s optimization]\n",
323 concurrency_mode == ConcurrencyMode::kConcurrent ? "concurrent"
324 : "non-concurrent");
325 }
326
327 // This function may not have been lazily compiled yet, even though its shared
328 // function has.
329 if (!function->is_compiled()) {
330 DCHECK(function->shared().IsInterpreted())((void) 0);
331 function->set_code(*BUILTIN_CODE(isolate, InterpreterEntryTrampoline)(isolate)->builtins()->builtin_handle(Builtins::kInterpreterEntryTrampoline
));
332 }
333
334 JSFunction::EnsureFeedbackVector(function, &is_compiled_scope);
335 function->MarkForOptimization(concurrency_mode);
336
337 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
338}
339
340namespace {
341
342bool EnsureFeedbackVector(Handle<JSFunction> function) {
343 // Check function allows lazy compilation.
344 if (!function->shared().allows_lazy_compilation()) return false;
345
346 if (function->has_feedback_vector()) return true;
347
348 // If function isn't compiled, compile it now.
349 IsCompiledScope is_compiled_scope(
350 function->shared().is_compiled_scope(function->GetIsolate()));
351 // If the JSFunction isn't compiled but it has a initialized feedback cell
352 // then no need to compile. CompileLazy builtin would handle these cases by
353 // installing the code from SFI. Calling compile here may cause another
354 // optimization if FLAG_always_opt is set.
355 bool needs_compilation =
356 !function->is_compiled() && !function->has_closure_feedback_cell_array();
357 if (needs_compilation &&
358 !Compiler::Compile(function, Compiler::CLEAR_EXCEPTION,
359 &is_compiled_scope)) {
360 return false;
361 }
362
363 // Ensure function has a feedback vector to hold type feedback for
364 // optimization.
365 JSFunction::EnsureFeedbackVector(function, &is_compiled_scope);
366 return true;
367}
368
369} // namespace
370

379RUNTIME_FUNCTION(Runtime_PrepareFunctionForOptimization)static inline __attribute__((always_inline)) Object __RT_impl_Runtime_PrepareFunctionForOptimization

))); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled379) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled379
= v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController
() ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled("disabled-by-default-" "v8.runtime"
); v8::base::Relaxed_Store(&(trace_event_unique_atomic379
), (reinterpret_cast<v8::base::AtomicWord>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled379
))); };; v8::internal::tracing::ScopedTracer trace_event_unique_tracer379

, trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled379, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_PrepareFunctionForOptimization", v8::internal::tracing
::kGlobalScope, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId, v8::internal::tracing

args(args_length, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_PrepareFunctionForOptimization
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } Address Runtime_PrepareFunctionForOptimization
(int args_length, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { (
(void) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled
()), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_PrepareFunctionForOptimization
(args_length, args_object, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(
args_length, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_PrepareFunctionForOptimization
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_PrepareFunctionForOptimization
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
380 HandleScope scope(isolate);
381 if ((args.length() != 1 && args.length() != 2) || !args[0].IsJSFunction()) {
382 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
383 }
384 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(JSFunction, function, 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0].IsJSFunction())), 0))
) { V8_Fatal("Check failed: %s.", "args[0].IsJSFunction()"); }
} while (false); Handle<JSFunction> function = args.at
<JSFunction>(0);;
385
386 bool allow_heuristic_optimization = false;
387 if (args.length() == 2) {
388 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, sync_object, 1)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[1].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[1].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> sync_object = args.at<Object>(1
);;
389 if (!sync_object->IsString()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
390 Handle<String> sync = Handle<String>::cast(sync_object);
391 if (sync->IsOneByteEqualTo(
392 StaticCharVector("allow heuristic optimization"))) {
393 allow_heuristic_optimization = true;
394 }
395 }
396
397 if (!EnsureFeedbackVector(function)) {
398 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
399 }
400
401 // If optimization is disabled for the function, return without making it
402 // pending optimize for test.
403 if (function->shared().optimization_disabled() &&
404 function->shared().disable_optimization_reason() ==
405 BailoutReason::kNeverOptimize) {
406 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
407 }
408
409 if (function->shared().HasAsmWasmData()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
410
411 // Hold onto the bytecode array between marking and optimization to ensure
412 // it's not flushed.
413 if (FLAG_testing_d8_test_runner) {
414 PendingOptimizationTable::PreparedForOptimization(
415 isolate, function, allow_heuristic_optimization);
416 }
417
418 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
419}

421RUNTIME_FUNCTION(Runtime_OptimizeOsr)static inline __attribute__((always_inline)) Object __RT_impl_Runtime_OptimizeOsr
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate); __attribute__((noinline
)) static Address Stats_Runtime_OptimizeOsr(int args_length, Address
* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { RuntimeCallTimerScope timer
(isolate, RuntimeCallCounterId::kRuntime_OptimizeOsr); static
v8::base::AtomicWord trace_event_unique_atomic421 = 0; const
uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled421; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled421
= reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(v8::base::Relaxed_Load
(&(trace_event_unique_atomic421))); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled421
) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled421 = v8::internal
::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController() ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled
("disabled-by-default-" "v8.runtime"); v8::base::Relaxed_Store
(&(trace_event_unique_atomic421), (reinterpret_cast<v8
::base::AtomicWord>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled421
))); };; v8::internal::tracing::ScopedTracer trace_event_unique_tracer421
; if (v8::base::Relaxed_Load(reinterpret_cast<const v8::base
::Atomic8*>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled421)
) & (kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags
)) { uint64_t h = v8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('X')
, trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled421, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_OptimizeOsr", v8::internal::tracing::kGlobalScope, v8
::internal::tracing::kNoId, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId, (static_cast
<unsigned int>(0))); trace_event_unique_tracer421 .Initialize
(trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled421, "V8.Runtime_" "Runtime_OptimizeOsr"
, h); }; RuntimeArguments args(args_length, args_object); return
(__RT_impl_Runtime_OptimizeOsr(args, isolate)).ptr(); } Address
Runtime_OptimizeOsr(int args_length, Address* args_object, Isolate
* isolate) { ((void) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags
::is_runtime_stats_enabled()), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_OptimizeOsr
(args_length, args_object, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(
args_length, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_OptimizeOsr
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_OptimizeOsr
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
422 HandleScope scope(isolate);
423 DCHECK(args.length() == 0 || args.length() == 1)((void) 0);
424
425 Handle<JSFunction> function;
426
427 // The optional parameter determines the frame being targeted.
428 int stack_depth = 0;
429 if (args.length() == 1) {
430 if (!args[0].IsSmi()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
431 stack_depth = args.smi_at(0);
432 }
433
434 // Find the JavaScript function on the top of the stack.
435 JavaScriptFrameIterator it(isolate);
436 while (!it.done() && stack_depth--) it.Advance();
437 if (!it.done()) function = handle(it.frame()->function(), isolate);
438 if (function.is_null()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
439
440 if (!FLAG_opt) return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
441
442 if (function->shared().optimization_disabled() &&
443 function->shared().disable_optimization_reason() ==
444 BailoutReason::kNeverOptimize) {
445 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
446 }
447
448 if (FLAG_testing_d8_test_runner) {
449 PendingOptimizationTable::MarkedForOptimization(isolate, function);
450 }
451
452 if (function->HasAvailableOptimizedCode()) {
453 DCHECK(function->HasAttachedOptimizedCode() ||((void) 0)
454 function->ChecksOptimizationMarker())((void) 0);
455 // If function is already optimized, remove the bytecode array from the
456 // pending optimize for test table and return.
457 if (FLAG_testing_d8_test_runner) {
458 PendingOptimizationTable::FunctionWasOptimized(isolate, function);
459 }
460 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
461 }
462
463 // Ensure that the function is marked for non-concurrent optimization, so that
464 // subsequent runs don't also optimize.
465 if (FLAG_trace_osr) {
466 CodeTracer::Scope scope(isolate->GetCodeTracer());
467 PrintF(scope.file(), "[OSR - OptimizeOsr marking ");
468 function->ShortPrint(scope.file());
469 PrintF(scope.file(), " for non-concurrent optimization]\n");
470 }
471 IsCompiledScope is_compiled_scope(
472 function->shared().is_compiled_scope(isolate));
473 JSFunction::EnsureFeedbackVector(function, &is_compiled_scope);
474 function->MarkForOptimization(ConcurrencyMode::kNotConcurrent);
475
476 // Make the profiler arm all back edges in unoptimized code.
477 if (it.frame()->type() == StackFrame::INTERPRETED) {
478 isolate->runtime_profiler()->AttemptOnStackReplacement(
479 InterpretedFrame::cast(it.frame()),
480 AbstractCode::kMaxLoopNestingMarker);
481 }
482
483 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
484}

488 HandleScope scope(isolate);

490 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, function_object, 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[0].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> function_object = args.at<Object>
(0);;
491 if (!function_object->IsJSFunction()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);

502RUNTIME_FUNCTION(Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus)static inline __attribute__((always_inline)) Object __RT_impl_Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate); __attribute__((noinline
)) static Address Stats_Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus(int args_length
, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { RuntimeCallTimerScope
timer(isolate, RuntimeCallCounterId::kRuntime_GetOptimizationStatus
); static v8::base::AtomicWord trace_event_unique_atomic502 =
0; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled502
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled502 = reinterpret_cast
<const uint8_t*>(v8::base::Relaxed_Load(&(trace_event_unique_atomic502
))); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled502) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled502
= v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController
() ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled("disabled-by-default-" "v8.runtime"
); v8::base::Relaxed_Store(&(trace_event_unique_atomic502
), (reinterpret_cast<v8::base::AtomicWord>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled502
))); };; v8::internal::tracing::ScopedTracer trace_event_unique_tracer502
; if (v8::base::Relaxed_Load(reinterpret_cast<const v8::base
::Atomic8*>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled502)
) & (kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags
)) { uint64_t h = v8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('X')
, trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled502, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus", v8::internal::tracing::kGlobalScope
, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId,
(static_cast<unsigned int>(0))); trace_event_unique_tracer502
.Initialize(trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled502, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus", h); }; RuntimeArguments args
(args_length, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } Address Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus
(int args_length, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { (
(void) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled
()), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus(args_length
, args_object, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(args_length,
args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_GetOptimizationStatus
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
503 HandleScope scope(isolate);
504 DCHECK(args.length() == 1 || args.length() == 2)((void) 0);
505 int status = 0;
506 if (FLAG_lite_mode || FLAG_jitless) {
507 // Both jitless and lite modes cannot optimize. Unit tests should handle
508 // these the same way. In the future, the two flags may become synonyms.
509 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kLiteMode);
510 }
511 if (!isolate->use_optimizer()) {
512 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kNeverOptimize);
513 }
514 if (FLAG_always_opt || FLAG_prepare_always_opt) {
515 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kAlwaysOptimize);
516 }
517 if (FLAG_deopt_every_n_times) {
518 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kMaybeDeopted);
519 }
520
521 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, function_object, 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[0].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> function_object = args.at<Object>
(0);;
522 if (function_object->IsUndefined()) return Smi::FromInt(status);
523 if (!function_object->IsJSFunction()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
524 Handle<JSFunction> function = Handle<JSFunction>::cast(function_object);
525
526 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kIsFunction);
527
528 bool sync_with_compiler_thread = true;
529 if (args.length() == 2) {
530 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, sync_object, 1)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[1].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[1].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> sync_object = args.at<Object>(1
);;
531 if (!sync_object->IsString()) return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
532 Handle<String> sync = Handle<String>::cast(sync_object);
533 if (sync->IsOneByteEqualTo(StaticCharVector("no sync"))) {
534 sync_with_compiler_thread = false;
535 } else if (sync->IsOneByteEqualTo(StaticCharVector("sync")) ||
536 sync->length() == 0) {
537 DCHECK(sync_with_compiler_thread)((void) 0);
538 } else {
539 return CrashUnlessFuzzing(isolate);
540 }
541 }
542
543 if (isolate->concurrent_recompilation_enabled() &&
544 sync_with_compiler_thread) {
545 while (function->IsInOptimizationQueue()) {
546 isolate->optimizing_compile_dispatcher()->InstallOptimizedFunctions();
547 base::OS::Sleep(base::TimeDelta::FromMilliseconds(50));
548 }
549 }
550
551 if (function->IsMarkedForOptimization()) {
552 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kMarkedForOptimization);
553 } else if (function->IsInOptimizationQueue()) {
554 status |=
555 static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kMarkedForConcurrentOptimization);
556 } else if (function->IsInOptimizationQueue()) {
557 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kOptimizingConcurrently);
558 }
559
560 if (function->HasAttachedOptimizedCode()) {
561 if (function->code().marked_for_deoptimization()) {
562 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kMarkedForDeoptimization);
563 } else {
564 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kOptimized);
565 }
566 if (function->code().is_turbofanned()) {
567 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kTurboFanned);
568 }
569 }
570 if (function->ActiveTierIsIgnition()) {
571 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kInterpreted);
572 }
573
574 // Additionally, detect activations of this frame on the stack, and report the
575 // status of the topmost frame.
576 JavaScriptFrame* frame = nullptr;
577 JavaScriptFrameIterator it(isolate);
578 while (!it.done()) {
579 if (it.frame()->function() == *function) {
580 frame = it.frame();
581 break;
582 }
583 it.Advance();
584 }
585 if (frame != nullptr) {
586 status |= static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kIsExecuting);
587 if (frame->is_optimized()) {
588 status |=
589 static_cast<int>(OptimizationStatus::kTopmostFrameIsTurboFanned);
590 }
591 }
592
593 return Smi::FromInt(status);
594}

619
620static void call_as_function(const v8::FunctionCallbackInfo<v8::Value>& args) {
621 double v1 =
622 args[0]->NumberValue(args.GetIsolate()->GetCurrentContext()).ToChecked();
623 double v2 =
624 args[1]->NumberValue(args.GetIsolate()->GetCurrentContext()).ToChecked();
625 args.GetReturnValue().Set(v8::Number::New(args.GetIsolate(), v1 - v2));
626}

))); };; v8::internal::tracing::ScopedTracer trace_event_unique_tracer630

Runtime_GetCallable(int args_length, Address* args_object, Isolate
* isolate) { ((void) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags

631 HandleScope scope(isolate);

634 Local<v8::FunctionTemplate> t = v8::FunctionTemplate::New(v8_isolate);
635 Local<ObjectTemplate> instance_template = t->InstanceTemplate();
636 instance_template->SetCallAsFunctionHandler(call_as_function);

640 .ToLocalChecked()

646RUNTIME_FUNCTION(Runtime_ClearFunctionFeedback)static inline __attribute__((always_inline)) Object __RT_impl_Runtime_ClearFunctionFeedback

, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { RuntimeCallTimerScope

); static v8::base::AtomicWord trace_event_unique_atomic646 =
0; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled646
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled646 = reinterpret_cast

697 if (inline_allocation) {
698 isolate->heap()->EnableInlineAllocation();
699 } else {
700 isolate->heap()->DisableInlineAllocation();
701 }
702 }
703#endif
704 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();

706
707namespace {
708
709int FixedArrayLenFromSize(int size) {
710 return Min((size - FixedArray::kHeaderSize) / kTaggedSize,
711 FixedArray::kMaxRegularLength);
712}
713
714void FillUpOneNewSpacePage(Isolate* isolate, Heap* heap) {
715 PauseAllocationObserversScope pause_observers(heap);
716 NewSpace* space = heap->new_space();
717 // We cannot rely on `space->limit()` to point to the end of the current page
718 // in the case where inline allocations are disabled, it actually points to
719 // the current allocation pointer.
720 DCHECK_IMPLIES(space->heap()->inline_allocation_disabled(),((void) 0)
721 space->limit() == space->top())((void) 0);
722 int space_remaining =
723 static_cast<int>(space->to_space().page_high() - space->top());
724 while (space_remaining > 0) {
725 int length = FixedArrayLenFromSize(space_remaining);
726 if (length > 0) {
727 Handle<FixedArray> padding =
728 isolate->factory()->NewFixedArray(length, AllocationType::kYoung);
729 DCHECK(heap->new_space()->Contains(*padding))((void) 0);
730 space_remaining -= padding->Size();
731 } else {
732 // Not enough room to create another fixed array. Create a filler.
733 heap->CreateFillerObjectAt(*heap->new_space()->allocation_top_address(),
734 space_remaining, ClearRecordedSlots::kNo);
735 break;
736 }
737 }
738}
739
740} // namespace

753
754static void DebugPrintImpl(MaybeObject maybe_object) {
755 StdoutStream os;
756 if (maybe_object->IsCleared()) {
757 os << "[weak cleared]";
758 } else {
759 Object object = maybe_object.GetHeapObjectOrSmi();
760 bool weak = maybe_object.IsWeak();
761
762#ifdef OBJECT_PRINT1
763 os << "DebugPrint: ";
764 if (weak) os << "[weak] ";
765 object.Print(os);
766 if (object.IsHeapObject()) {
767 HeapObject::cast(object).map().Print(os);
768 }
769#else
770 if (weak) os << "[weak] ";
771 // ShortPrint is available in release mode. Print is not.
772 os << Brief(object);
773#endif
774 }
775 os << std::endl;
776}

; return (__RT_impl_Runtime_DebugPrintPtr(args, isolate)).ptr
(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_DebugPrintPtr(RuntimeArguments
args, Isolate* isolate) {
788 SealHandleScope shs(isolate);
789 StdoutStream os;
790 DCHECK_EQ(1, args.length())((void) 0);
791
792 MaybeObject maybe_object(*args.address_of_arg_at(0));
793 if (!maybe_object.IsCleared()) {
794 Object object = maybe_object.GetHeapObjectOrSmi();
795 size_t pointer;
796 if (object.ToIntegerIndex(&pointer)) {
797 MaybeObject from_pointer(static_cast<Address>(pointer));
798 DebugPrintImpl(from_pointer);
799 }
800 }
801 // We don't allow the converted pointer to leak out to JavaScript.
802 return args[0];
803}

942namespace {
943
944int StackSize(Isolate* isolate) {
945 int n = 0;
946 for (JavaScriptFrameIterator it(isolate); !it.done(); it.Advance()) n++;
947 return n;
948}
949
950void PrintIndentation(int stack_size) {
951 const int max_display = 80;
952 if (stack_size <= max_display) {
953 PrintF("%4d:%*s", stack_size, stack_size, "");
954 } else {
955 PrintF("%4d:%*s", stack_size, max_display, "...");
956 }
957}

983int WasmStackSize(Isolate* isolate) {
984 // TODO(wasm): Fix this for mixed JS/Wasm stacks with both --trace and
985 // --trace-wasm.
986 int n = 0;
987 for (StackTraceFrameIterator it(isolate); !it.done(); it.Advance()) {
988 if (it.is_wasm()) n++;
989 }
990 return n;
991}

995RUNTIME_FUNCTION(Runtime_WasmTraceEnter)static inline __attribute__((always_inline)) Object __RT_impl_Runtime_WasmTraceEnter
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate); __attribute__((noinline
)) static Address Stats_Runtime_WasmTraceEnter(int args_length
, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { RuntimeCallTimerScope
timer(isolate, RuntimeCallCounterId::kRuntime_WasmTraceEnter
); static v8::base::AtomicWord trace_event_unique_atomic995 =
0; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled995
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled995 = reinterpret_cast
<const uint8_t*>(v8::base::Relaxed_Load(&(trace_event_unique_atomic995
))); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled995) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled995
= v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController
() ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled("disabled-by-default-" "v8.runtime"
); v8::base::Relaxed_Store(&(trace_event_unique_atomic995
), (reinterpret_cast<v8::base::AtomicWord>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled995
))); };; v8::internal::tracing::ScopedTracer trace_event_unique_tracer995
; if (v8::base::Relaxed_Load(reinterpret_cast<const v8::base
::Atomic8*>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled995)
) & (kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags
)) { uint64_t h = v8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('X')
, trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled995, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_WasmTraceEnter", v8::internal::tracing::kGlobalScope
, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId,
(static_cast<unsigned int>(0))); trace_event_unique_tracer995
.Initialize(trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled995, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_WasmTraceEnter", h); }; RuntimeArguments args(args_length
, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_WasmTraceEnter(args
, isolate)).ptr(); } Address Runtime_WasmTraceEnter(int args_length
, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { ((void) 0); ; if (
(__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled()
), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_WasmTraceEnter(args_length, args_object
, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(args_length, args_object)
; return (__RT_impl_Runtime_WasmTraceEnter(args, isolate)).ptr
(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_WasmTraceEnter(RuntimeArguments
args, Isolate* isolate) {
996 HandleScope shs(isolate);
997 DCHECK_EQ(0, args.length())((void) 0);
998 PrintIndentation(WasmStackSize(isolate));
999
1000 // Find the caller wasm frame.
1001 wasm::WasmCodeRefScope wasm_code_ref_scope;
1002 StackTraceFrameIterator it(isolate);
1003 DCHECK(!it.done())((void) 0);
1004 DCHECK(it.is_wasm())((void) 0);
1005 WasmFrame* frame = WasmFrame::cast(it.frame());
1006
1007 // Find the function name.
1008 int func_index = frame->function_index();
1009 const wasm::WasmModule* module = frame->wasm_instance().module();
1010 wasm::ModuleWireBytes wire_bytes =
1011 wasm::ModuleWireBytes(frame->native_module()->wire_bytes());
1012 wasm::WireBytesRef name_ref =
1013 module->lazily_generated_names.LookupFunctionName(
1014 wire_bytes, func_index, VectorOf(module->export_table));
1015 wasm::WasmName name = wire_bytes.GetNameOrNull(name_ref);
1016
1017 wasm::WasmCode* code = frame->wasm_code();
1018 PrintF(code->is_liftoff() ? "~" : "*");
1019
1020 if (name.empty()) {
1021 PrintF("wasm-function[%d] {\n", func_index);
1022 } else {
1023 PrintF("wasm-function[%d] \"%.*s\" {\n", func_index, name.length(),
1024 name.begin());
1025 }
1026
1027 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
1028}

1030RUNTIME_FUNCTION(Runtime_WasmTraceExit)static inline __attribute__((always_inline)) Object __RT_impl_Runtime_WasmTraceExit
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate); __attribute__((noinline
)) static Address Stats_Runtime_WasmTraceExit(int args_length
, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { RuntimeCallTimerScope
timer(isolate, RuntimeCallCounterId::kRuntime_WasmTraceExit)

), (reinterpret_cast<v8::base::AtomicWord>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1030

)) & (kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags
)) { uint64_t h = v8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('X')
, trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1030, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_WasmTraceExit", v8::internal::tracing::kGlobalScope
, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId,

.Initialize(trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1030, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_WasmTraceExit", h); }; RuntimeArguments args(args_length
, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_WasmTraceExit(args,
isolate)).ptr(); } Address Runtime_WasmTraceExit(int args_length
, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { ((void) 0); ; if (
(__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled()
), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_WasmTraceExit(args_length, args_object
, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(args_length, args_object)
; return (__RT_impl_Runtime_WasmTraceExit(args, isolate)).ptr
(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_WasmTraceExit(RuntimeArguments
args, Isolate* isolate) {
1031 HandleScope shs(isolate);
1032 DCHECK_EQ(1, args.length())((void) 0);
1033 CONVERT_ARG_CHECKED(Smi, value_addr_smi, 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0].IsSmi())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[0].IsSmi()"); } } while (false); Smi
value_addr_smi = Smi::cast(args[0]);;
1034
1035 PrintIndentation(WasmStackSize(isolate));
1036 PrintF("}");
1037
1038 // Find the caller wasm frame.
1039 wasm::WasmCodeRefScope wasm_code_ref_scope;
1040 StackTraceFrameIterator it(isolate);
1041 DCHECK(!it.done())((void) 0);
1042 DCHECK(it.is_wasm())((void) 0);
1043 WasmFrame* frame = WasmFrame::cast(it.frame());
1044 int func_index = frame->function_index();
1045 const wasm::FunctionSig* sig =
1046 frame->wasm_instance().module()->functions[func_index].sig;
1047
1048 size_t num_returns = sig->return_count();
1049 if (num_returns == 1) {
1050 wasm::ValueType return_type = sig->GetReturn(0);
1051 switch (return_type.kind()) {
1052 case wasm::ValueType::kI32: {
1053 int32_t value = ReadUnalignedValue<int32_t>(value_addr_smi.ptr());
1054 PrintF(" -> %d\n", value);
1055 break;
1056 }
1057 case wasm::ValueType::kI64: {
1058 int64_t value = ReadUnalignedValue<int64_t>(value_addr_smi.ptr());
1059 PrintF(" -> %" PRId64"l" "d" "\n", value);
1060 break;
1061 }
1062 case wasm::ValueType::kF32: {
1063 float_t value = ReadUnalignedValue<float_t>(value_addr_smi.ptr());
1064 PrintF(" -> %f\n", value);
1065 break;
1066 }
1067 case wasm::ValueType::kF64: {
1068 double_t value = ReadUnalignedValue<double_t>(value_addr_smi.ptr());
1069 PrintF(" -> %f\n", value);
1070 break;
1071 }
1072 default:
1073 PrintF(" -> Unsupported type\n");
1074 break;
1075 }
1076 } else {
1077 // TODO(wasm) Handle multiple return values.
1078 PrintF("\n");
1079 }
1080
1081 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
1082}

1354// Take an array buffer and attempt to reconstruct a compiled wasm module.

1356RUNTIME_FUNCTION(Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule)static inline __attribute__((always_inline)) Object __RT_impl_Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate); __attribute__((noinline
)) static Address Stats_Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule(int args_length
, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { RuntimeCallTimerScope

), (reinterpret_cast<v8::base::AtomicWord>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1356
))); };; v8::internal::tracing::ScopedTracer trace_event_unique_tracer1356

)) & (kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags

, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId, v8::internal::tracing::kNoId,

.Initialize(trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1356, "V8.Runtime_"
"Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule", h); }; RuntimeArguments args
(args_length, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } Address Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule
(int args_length, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { (
(void) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled
()), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule(args_length
, args_object, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(args_length,
args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_DeserializeWasmModule
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
1357 HandleScope scope(isolate);
1358 DCHECK_EQ(2, args.length())((void) 0);
1359 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(JSArrayBuffer, buffer, 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0].IsJSArrayBuffer())), 0
))) { V8_Fatal("Check failed: %s.", "args[0].IsJSArrayBuffer()"
); } } while (false); Handle<JSArrayBuffer> buffer = args
.at<JSArrayBuffer>(0);;
1360 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(JSTypedArray, wire_bytes, 1)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[1].IsJSTypedArray())), 0
))) { V8_Fatal("Check failed: %s.", "args[1].IsJSTypedArray()"
); } } while (false); Handle<JSTypedArray> wire_bytes =
args.at<JSTypedArray>(1);;
1361 CHECK(!buffer->was_detached())do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(!buffer->was_detached())),
0))) { V8_Fatal("Check failed: %s.", "!buffer->was_detached()"
); } } while (false);
1362 CHECK(!wire_bytes->WasDetached())do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(!wire_bytes->WasDetached()
)), 0))) { V8_Fatal("Check failed: %s.", "!wire_bytes->WasDetached()"
); } } while (false);
1363
1364 Handle<JSArrayBuffer> wire_bytes_buffer = wire_bytes->GetBuffer();
1365 Vector<const uint8_t> wire_bytes_vec{
1366 reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(wire_bytes_buffer->backing_store()) +
1367 wire_bytes->byte_offset(),
1368 wire_bytes->byte_length()};
1369 Vector<uint8_t> buffer_vec{
1370 reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(buffer->backing_store()),
1371 buffer->byte_length()};
1372
1373 // Note that {wasm::DeserializeNativeModule} will allocate. We assume the
1374 // JSArrayBuffer backing store doesn't get relocated.
1375 MaybeHandle<WasmModuleObject> maybe_module_object =
1376 wasm::DeserializeNativeModule(isolate, buffer_vec, wire_bytes_vec, {});
1377 Handle<WasmModuleObject> module_object;
1378 if (!maybe_module_object.ToHandle(&module_object)) {
1379 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
1380 }
1381 return *module_object;

(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
1554 // The {NoopListener} currently does nothing on any callback, but reports
1555 // {true} on {is_listening_to_code_events()}. Feel free to add assertions to
1556 // any method to further test the code logging callbacks.
1557 class NoopListener final : public CodeEventListener {
1558 void CodeCreateEvent(LogEventsAndTags tag, Handle<AbstractCode> code,
1559 const char* name) final {}
1560 void CodeCreateEvent(LogEventsAndTags tag, Handle<AbstractCode> code,
1561 Handle<Name> name) final {}
1562 void CodeCreateEvent(LogEventsAndTags tag, Handle<AbstractCode> code,
1563 Handle<SharedFunctionInfo> shared,
1564 Handle<Name> script_name) final {}
1565 void CodeCreateEvent(LogEventsAndTags tag, Handle<AbstractCode> code,
1566 Handle<SharedFunctionInfo> shared,
1567 Handle<Name> script_name, int line, int column) final {
1568 }
1569 void CodeCreateEvent(LogEventsAndTags tag, const wasm::WasmCode* code,
1570 wasm::WasmName name) final {}
1571
1572 void CallbackEvent(Handle<Name> name, Address entry_point) final {}
1573 void GetterCallbackEvent(Handle<Name> name, Address entry_point) final {}
1574 void SetterCallbackEvent(Handle<Name> name, Address entry_point) final {}
1575 void RegExpCodeCreateEvent(Handle<AbstractCode> code,
1576 Handle<String> source) final {}
1577 void CodeMoveEvent(AbstractCode from, AbstractCode to) final {}
1578 void SharedFunctionInfoMoveEvent(Address from, Address to) final {}
1579 void NativeContextMoveEvent(Address from, Address to) final {}
1580 void CodeMovingGCEvent() final {}
1581 void CodeDisableOptEvent(Handle<AbstractCode> code,
1582 Handle<SharedFunctionInfo> shared) final {}
1583 void CodeDeoptEvent(Handle<Code> code, DeoptimizeKind kind, Address pc,
1584 int fp_to_sp_delta, bool reuse_code) final {}
1585 void CodeDependencyChangeEvent(Handle<Code> code,
1586 Handle<SharedFunctionInfo> shared,
1587 const char* reason) final {}
1588
1589 bool is_listening_to_code_events() final { return true; }
1590 };
1591 static base::LeakyObject<NoopListener> noop_listener;
1592 isolate->wasm_engine()->EnableCodeLogging(isolate);
1593 isolate->code_event_dispatcher()->AddListener(noop_listener.get());
1594 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).undefined_value();
1595}
